class TestExtractPdfDataEndpoint:
    """Testes para o endpoint /extract-pdf-data."""
    
    @patch('app.controller.processamento_controller.convert_pdf_to_images_and_extract_data')
    def test_extract_pdf_data_success(self, mock_convert, client):
        """Testa upload e extração bem-sucedida de PDF."""
        # Arrange
        mock_convert.return_value = (
            {"acidez": "0.5", "peroxidos": "10.2"},
            {"lote": "L123", "laboratorio": "Lab Test"}
        )
        
        pdf_content = b"%PDF-1.4 test content"
        files = {"laudo": ("test.pdf", pdf_content, "application/pdf")}
        data = {"lpco": "BR2025123456"}
        
        # Act
        response = client.post("/extract-pdf-data", files=files, data=data)
        
        # Assert
        assert response.status_code == 200
        result = response.json()
        assert "quimico" in result
        assert "cabecalho" in result
        assert result["quimico"]["acidez"] == "0.5"
        assert result["cabecalho"]["lote"] == "L123"
        
        mock_convert.assert_called_once()
        # Verificar parâmetros da chamada
        call_args = mock_convert.call_args
        assert "BR2025123456" in call_args[0][1]  # lpco in file path
    
    def test_extract_pdf_data_missing_lpco(self, client):
        """Testa erro quando LPCO não é fornecido."""
        # Arrange
        pdf_content = b"%PDF-1.4 test content"
        files = {"laudo": ("test.pdf", pdf_content, "application/pdf")}
        
        # Act
        response = client.post("/extract-pdf-data", files=files)
        
        # Assert
        assert response.status_code == 422  # Validation error
    
    def test_extract_pdf_data_missing_file(self, client):
        """Testa erro quando arquivo PDF não é fornecido."""
        # Arrange
        data = {"lpco": "BR2025123456"}
        
        # Act
        response = client.post("/extract-pdf-data", data=data)
        
        # Assert
        assert response.status_code == 422  # Validation error
    
    @patch('app.controller.processamento_controller.convert_pdf_to_images_and_extract_data')
    def test_extract_pdf_data_processing_error(self, mock_convert, client):
        """Testa tratamento de erro durante processamento."""
        # Arrange
        mock_convert.side_effect = RuntimeError("Processing failed")
        
        files = {"laudo": ("test.pdf", b"content", "application/pdf")}
        data = {"lpco": "TEST123"}
        
        # Act
        response = client.post("/extract-pdf-data", files=files, data=data)
        
        # Assert
        assert response.status_code == 500
    
    @patch('app.controller.processamento_controller.convert_pdf_to_images_and_extract_data')
    def test_extract_pdf_data_invalid_file_error(self, mock_convert, client):
        """Testa erro de arquivo inválido (HTTPException 400)."""
        # Arrange
        from fastapi import HTTPException
        mock_convert.side_effect = HTTPException(status_code=400, detail="Arquivo inválido")
        
        files = {"laudo": ("test.pdf", b"content", "application/pdf")}
        data = {"lpco": "TEST123"}
        
        # Act
        response = client.post("/extract-pdf-data", files=files, data=data)
        
        # Assert
        assert response.status_code == 400
        assert "Arquivo inválido" in response.json()["detail"]


class TestDataProcessingEndpoint:
    """Testes para o endpoint assíncrono /data-processing."""
    
    @patch("main.create_sheets_and_save_pdf")
    def test_data_processing_success(self, mock_create, client):
        """Testa processamento bem-sucedido de dados extraídos."""
        # Arrange
        from fastapi.responses import FileResponse
        from fastapi import BackgroundTasks
        
        # Mock FileResponse - return a simple dict since the endpoint returns the result directly
        mock_response = {"status": "success", "file": "test.pdf"}
        mock_create.return_value = mock_response
        
        request_data = {
            "lpco": "TEST123",
            "chem_data": {"acidez": "0.5", "peroxidos": "10.2"},
            "sec_data": {"lote": "L123", "laboratorio": "Lab Test"}
        }
        
        # Act
        response = client.post("/data-processing", json=request_data)
        
        # Assert
        assert response.status_code == 200
        mock_create.assert_called_once_with(
            "TEST123",
            {"acidez": "0.5", "peroxidos": "10.2"},
            {"lote": "L123", "laboratorio": "Lab Test"}
        )
    
    def test_data_processing_missing_lpco(self, client):
        """Testa erro quando LPCO está ausente."""
        # Arrange
        request_data = {
            "chem_data": {"acidez": "0.5"},
            "sec_data": {"lote": "L123"}
        }
        
        # Act
        response = client.post("/data-processing", json=request_data)
        
        # Assert
        assert response.status_code == 200
        result = response.json()
        assert "error" in result
        assert "Campo 'lpco' obrigatório" in result["error"]
    
    def test_data_processing_invalid_lpco_type(self, client):
        """Testa erro quando LPCO não é string."""
        # Arrange
        request_data = {
            "lpco": 123,  # Número em vez de string
            "chem_data": {"acidez": "0.5"},
            "sec_data": {"lote": "L123"}
        }
        
        # Act
        response = client.post("/data-processing", json=request_data)
        
        # Assert
        assert response.status_code == 200
        result = response.json()
        assert "error" in result
        assert "deve ser string" in result["error"]
    
    def test_data_processing_missing_chem_data(self, client):
        """Testa erro quando chem_data está ausente."""
        # Arrange
        request_data = {
            "lpco": "TEST123",
            "sec_data": {"lote": "L123"}
        }
        
        # Act
        response = client.post("/data-processing", json=request_data)
        
        # Assert
        assert response.status_code == 200
        result = response.json()
        assert "error" in result
        assert "Campo 'chem_data' obrigatório" in result["error"]
    
    def test_data_processing_missing_sec_data(self, client):
        """Testa erro quando sec_data está ausente."""
        # Arrange
        request_data = {
            "lpco": "TEST123",
            "chem_data": {"acidez": "0.5"}
        }
        
        # Act
        response = client.post("/data-processing", json=request_data)
        
        # Assert
        assert response.status_code == 200
        result = response.json()
        assert "error" in result
        assert "Campo 'sec_data' obrigatório" in result["error"]
    
    def test_data_processing_null_values(self, client):
        """Testa tratamento de valores null nos dados."""
        # Arrange
        request_data = {
            "lpco": "TEST123",
            "chem_data": None,
            "sec_data": None
        }
        
        # Act
        response = client.post("/data-processing", json=request_data)
        
        # Assert
        assert response.status_code == 200
        result = response.json()
        assert "error" in result
    
    @patch("main.create_sheets_and_save_pdf")
    def test_data_processing_controller_exception(self, mock_create, client):
        """Testa tratamento de exceção durante processamento."""
        # Arrange
        mock_create.side_effect = Exception("Processing error")
        
        request_data = {
            "lpco": "TEST123",
            "chem_data": {"acidez": "0.5"},
            "sec_data": {"lote": "L123"}
        }
        
        # Act
        response = client.post("/data-processing", json=request_data)
        
        # Assert
        assert response.status_code == 500
    
    def test_data_processing_empty_data_structures(self, client):
        """Testa processamento com estruturas de dados vazias mas válidas."""
        # Arrange
        with patch('main.create_sheets_and_save_pdf') as mock_create:
            mock_create.return_value = {"status": "success", "file": "test.pdf"}
            
            request_data = {
                "lpco": "TEST123",
                "chem_data": {},
                "sec_data": {}
            }
            
            # Act
            response = client.post("/data-processing", json=request_data)
            
            # Assert
            assert response.status_code == 200
            mock_create.assert_called_once_with("TEST123", {}, {})


class TestCorsMiddleware:
    """Testes para configuração CORS da API."""
    
    def test_cors_headers_present(self, client):
        """Testa se headers CORS estão presentes na resposta."""
        # Act - Add Origin header to trigger CORS
        response = client.get("/", headers={"Origin": "http://localhost:3000"})
        
        # Assert
        assert response.status_code == 200
        headers = response.headers
        
        # Verificar headers CORS principais
        assert "access-control-allow-origin" in headers
        assert headers["access-control-allow-origin"] == "*"
    
    def test_cors_allows_all_origins(self, client):
        """Testa se CORS permite todas as origens (configuração atual)."""
        # Act
        response = client.get("/", headers={"Origin": "http://localhost:3000"})
        
        # Assert
        assert response.status_code == 200
        assert response.headers.get("access-control-allow-origin") == "*"
    
    def test_preflight_request(self, client):
        """Testa requisição preflight OPTIONS."""
        # Act
        response = client.options(
            "/extract-pdf-data",
            headers={
                "Origin": "http://localhost:3000",
                "Access-Control-Request-Method": "POST",
                "Access-Control-Request-Headers": "Content-Type"
            }
        )
        
        # Assert
        assert response.status_code == 200


class TestStaticFileServing:
    """Testes para servimento de arquivos estáticos."""
    
    def test_static_mount_configured(self, client):
        """Testa se mount de arquivos estáticos está configurado."""
        # Act - tentar acessar diretório de laudos (mesmo que vazio)
        response = client.get("/laudos/")
        
        # Assert - deve retornar 404 (diretório vazio) ou 403 (sem permissão de listagem)
        # mas não 500 (erro de configuração)
        assert response.status_code in [403, 404, 200]
    
    @patch('os.path.exists')
    def test_static_file_access(self, mock_exists, client, temp_dir):
        """Testa acesso a arquivo estático existente."""
        # Arrange
        mock_exists.return_value = True
        
        # Criar arquivo temporário no diretório de laudos
        test_file = temp_dir / "test-laudo.pdf"
        test_file.write_bytes(b"PDF content")
        
        with patch('fastapi.staticfiles.StaticFiles') as mock_static:
            # Act
            response = client.get("/laudos/test-laudo.pdf")
            
            # Assert - verifica que a configuração está correta
            # (o resultado específico depende da configuração do StaticFiles)
            assert response.status_code != 500  # Não deve ser erro de configuração


class TestErrorHandling:
    """Testes para tratamento de erros gerais da API."""
    
    def test_invalid_json_request(self, client):
        """Testa tratamento de JSON inválido."""
        # Act
        response = client.post(
            "/data-processing",
            content="invalid json",
            headers={"Content-Type": "application/json"}
        )
        
        # Assert
        assert response.status_code == 500  # Internal Server Error due to JSON parsing failure
    
    def test_large_file_upload(self, client):
        """Testa comportamento com arquivo muito grande."""
        # Arrange - criar arquivo de 10MB
        large_content = b"x" * (10 * 1024 * 1024)
        files = {"laudo": ("large.pdf", large_content, "application/pdf")}
        data = {"lpco": "LARGE_TEST"}
        
        # Act
        response = client.post("/extract-pdf-data", files=files, data=data)
        
        # Assert - pode falhar por tamanho ou ser processado normalmente
        assert response.status_code in [200, 413, 422, 500]  # Respostas válidas
    
    def test_malformed_multipart_request(self, client):
        """Testa requisição multipart malformada."""
        # Act
        response = client.post(
            "/extract-pdf-data",
            content=b"malformed multipart data",
            headers={"Content-Type": "multipart/form-data"}
        )
        
        # Assert
        assert response.status_code == 400  # Bad Request for malformed multipart


# Testes de integração end-to-end
class TestEndToEndFlow:
    """Testes de integração completa da API."""
    
    @patch('app.controller.processamento_controller.convert_pdf_to_images_and_extract_data')
    @patch('main.create_sheets_and_save_pdf')
    def test_complete_api_flow(self, mock_create, mock_ai_extract, client):
        """Testa fluxo completo: upload → extração → processamento → download."""
        # Arrange
        mock_ai_extract.return_value = (
            {"acidez": "0.5", "peroxidos": "10.2"},
            {"lote": "L123", "laboratorio": "Test Lab"}
        )
        
        # Etapa 1: Upload e extração
        files = {"laudo": ("test.pdf", b"%PDF-1.4 test", "application/pdf")}
        data = {"lpco": "E2E_TEST"}
        
        extract_response = client.post("/extract-pdf-data", files=files, data=data)
        
        # Assert Etapa 1
        assert extract_response.status_code == 200
        extract_data = extract_response.json()
        
        # Etapa 2: Processamento
        mock_create.return_value = {"status": "success", "file": "test.pdf"}
        
        process_data = {
            "lpco": "E2E_TEST",
            "chem_data": extract_data["quimico"],
            "sec_data": extract_data["cabecalho"]
        }
        
        process_response = client.post("/data-processing", json=process_data)
        
        # Assert Etapa 2
        assert process_response.status_code == 200
        
        # Verificar que todo o fluxo foi executado
        mock_ai_extract.assert_called_once()
        mock_create.assert_called_once()
    
    @patch('app.controller.processamento_controller.convert_pdf_to_images_and_extract_data')
    def test_error_in_extraction_stops_flow(self, mock_extract, client):
        """Testa que erro na extração impede o fluxo de continuar."""
        # Arrange - forçar erro com arquivo inválido
        from fastapi import HTTPException
        mock_extract.side_effect = HTTPException(status_code=400, detail="Invalid file")
        
        files = {"laudo": ("invalid.txt", b"not pdf", "application/pdf")}
        data = {"lpco": "ERROR_TEST"}
        
        # Act
        response = client.post("/extract-pdf-data", files=files, data=data)
        
        # Assert
        assert response.status_code == 400
        # Fluxo deve parar aqui - não tentar processar dados inválidos"""Testes para OCRService - Serviço de OCR com correção inteligente de texto."""

import pytest
import os
import tempfile
from unittest.mock import Mock, patch, MagicMock, mock_open
from PIL import Image
import numpy as np

from app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service import OCRService, get_ocr_service


class TestOCRServiceSingleton:
    """Testes para padrão singleton do OCRService."""
    
    def test_singleton_pattern(self):
        """Testa se OCRService implementa corretamente o padrão singleton."""
        # Reset singleton para teste limpo
        OCRService._instance = None
        OCRService._config = None
        OCRService._ocr_provider = None
        
        with patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.get_config'), \
             patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.get_file_manager'), \
             patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.get_ocr_provider'), \
             patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.ImageCorrector'), \
             patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.DataConsolidator'):
            
            service1 = OCRService()
            service2 = OCRService()
            
            assert service1 is service2
            assert OCRService._instance is service1
    
    def test_get_ocr_service_function(self):
        """Testa função global get_ocr_service."""
        # Reset singleton
        OCRService._instance = None
        OCRService._config = None
        OCRService._ocr_provider = None
        
        with patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.get_config'), \
             patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.get_file_manager'), \
             patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.get_ocr_provider'), \
             patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.ImageCorrector'), \
             patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.DataConsolidator'):
            
            service = get_ocr_service()
            assert isinstance(service, OCRService)


class TestOCRServiceInit:
    """Testes para inicialização do OCRService."""
    
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.DataConsolidator')
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.ImageCorrector')
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.get_ocr_provider')
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.get_file_manager')
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.get_config')
    def test_successful_initialization(self, mock_get_config, mock_get_file_manager,
                                     mock_get_ocr_provider, mock_image_corrector,
                                     mock_data_consolidator):
        """Testa inicialização bem-sucedida do OCRService."""
        # Reset singleton
        OCRService._instance = None
        OCRService._config = None
        OCRService._ocr_provider = None
        
        # Setup mocks
        mock_config = Mock()
        mock_config.ocr_provider = "easy"
        mock_config.debug_ocr = False
        mock_get_config.return_value = mock_config
        
        mock_provider = Mock()
        mock_provider.provider_name = "EasyOCR"
        mock_get_ocr_provider.return_value = mock_provider
        
        mock_file_manager = Mock()
        mock_get_file_manager.return_value = mock_file_manager
        
        with patch('builtins.print') as mock_print:
            service = OCRService()
            
            assert service._config is mock_config
            assert service.file_manager is mock_file_manager
            assert service._ocr_provider is mock_provider
            
            # Verificar chamadas de inicialização
            mock_get_ocr_provider.assert_called_with("easy")
            mock_image_corrector.assert_called_with(angle_threshold=1.0, debug=False)
            mock_data_consolidator.assert_called_with(debug=False)
            
            # Verificar mensagens de log
            mock_print.assert_any_call("[OCR] EasyOCR inicializado com sucesso")
            mock_print.assert_any_call("[OCR] Corretor de imagens inicializado")
            mock_print.assert_any_call("[OCR] Consolidador de dados inicializado")
    
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.DataConsolidator')
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.ImageCorrector')
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.get_ocr_provider')
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.get_file_manager')
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.get_config')
    def test_initialization_with_provider_error_fallback(self, mock_get_config, mock_get_file_manager,
                                                        mock_get_ocr_provider, mock_image_corrector,
                                                        mock_data_consolidator):
        """Testa inicialização com erro no provedor OCR e fallback."""
        # Reset singleton
        OCRService._instance = None
        OCRService._config = None
        OCRService._ocr_provider = None
        
        # Setup mocks
        mock_config = Mock()
        mock_config.ocr_provider = "invalid_provider"
        mock_config.debug_ocr = True
        mock_get_config.return_value = mock_config
        
        mock_fallback_provider = Mock()
        mock_fallback_provider.provider_name = "EasyOCR (Fallback)"
        
        # Primeiro erro, depois sucesso no fallback
        mock_get_ocr_provider.side_effect = [Exception("Provider error"), mock_fallback_provider]
        
        with patch('builtins.print') as mock_print:
            service = OCRService()
            
            # Verificar fallback foi acionado
            calls = mock_get_ocr_provider.call_args_list
            assert len(calls) == 2
            assert calls[0][0][0] == "invalid_provider"  # Primeira tentativa
            assert calls[1][0][0] == "easy"  # Fallback
            
            mock_print.assert_any_call("[OCR] Erro ao inicializar provedor OCR: Provider error")
            mock_print.assert_any_call("[OCR] Fallback para EasyOCR (Fallback)")
    
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.DataConsolidator')
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.ImageCorrector')
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.get_ocr_provider')
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.get_file_manager')
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.get_config')
    def test_initialization_complete_failure(self, mock_get_config, mock_get_file_manager,
                                           mock_get_ocr_provider, mock_image_corrector,
                                           mock_data_consolidator):
        """Testa inicialização quando tanto provedor quanto fallback falham."""
        # Reset singleton
        OCRService._instance = None
        OCRService._config = None
        OCRService._ocr_provider = None
        
        # Setup mocks
        mock_config = Mock()
        mock_config.ocr_provider = "invalid_provider"
        mock_get_config.return_value = mock_config
        
        # Ambos falham
        mock_get_ocr_provider.side_effect = Exception("Complete failure")
        
        with patch('builtins.print') as mock_print:
            service = OCRService()
            
            assert service._ocr_provider is None
            mock_print.assert_any_call("[OCR] Erro no fallback: Complete failure")


class TestOCRServiceProperties:
    """Testes para propriedades do OCRService."""
    
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.DataConsolidator')
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.ImageCorrector')
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.get_ocr_provider')
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.get_file_manager')
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.get_config')
    def test_reader_property_success(self, mock_get_config, mock_get_file_manager,
                                   mock_get_ocr_provider, mock_image_corrector,
                                   mock_data_consolidator):
        """Testa propriedade reader com provedor válido."""
        # Reset singleton
        OCRService._instance = None
        OCRService._config = None
        OCRService._ocr_provider = None
        
        mock_provider = Mock()
        mock_get_ocr_provider.return_value = mock_provider
        mock_get_config.return_value = Mock(ocr_provider="easy", debug_ocr=False)
        
        service = OCRService()
        assert service.reader is mock_provider
    
    def test_reader_property_no_provider(self):
        """Testa propriedade reader sem provedor válido."""
        # Reset singleton
        OCRService._instance = None
        OCRService._config = None
        OCRService._ocr_provider = None
        
        with patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.get_config'), \
             patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.get_file_manager'), \
             patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.get_ocr_provider', side_effect=Exception()), \
             patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.ImageCorrector'), \
             patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.DataConsolidator'), \
             patch('builtins.print'):
            
            service = OCRService()
            
            with pytest.raises(RuntimeError, match="Provedor OCR não foi inicializado corretamente"):
                _ = service.reader
    
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.DataConsolidator')
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.ImageCorrector')
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.get_ocr_provider')
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.get_file_manager')
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.get_config')
    def test_config_property(self, mock_get_config, mock_get_file_manager,
                           mock_get_ocr_provider, mock_image_corrector,
                           mock_data_consolidator):
        """Testa propriedade config."""
        # Reset singleton
        OCRService._instance = None
        OCRService._config = None
        OCRService._ocr_provider = None
        
        mock_config = Mock()
        mock_get_config.return_value = mock_config
        mock_get_ocr_provider.return_value = Mock()
        
        service = OCRService()
        assert service.config is mock_config


class TestConvertPdfToImages:
    """Testes para conversão de PDF para imagens."""
    
    def setup_method(self):
        """Setup para cada teste."""
        # Reset singleton
        OCRService._instance = None
        OCRService._config = None
        OCRService._ocr_provider = None
    
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.convert_from_path')
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.DataConsolidator')
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.ImageCorrector')
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.get_ocr_provider')
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.get_file_manager')
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.get_config')
    def test_convert_pdf_to_images_success(self, mock_get_config, mock_get_file_manager,
                                         mock_get_ocr_provider, mock_image_corrector,
                                         mock_data_consolidator, mock_convert):
        """Testa conversão bem-sucedida de PDF para imagens."""
        # Setup mocks
        mock_config = Mock()
        mock_config.dpi = 300
        mock_get_config.return_value = mock_config
        
        mock_file_manager = Mock()
        mock_file_manager.get_temp_image_path.side_effect = [
            "/tmp/page_1_LPCO123.png",
            "/tmp/page_2_LPCO123.png"
        ]
        mock_get_file_manager.return_value = mock_file_manager
        
        mock_get_ocr_provider.return_value = Mock()
        
        # Criar imagens PIL mock
        mock_image1 = Mock(spec=Image.Image)
        mock_image2 = Mock(spec=Image.Image)
        mock_convert.return_value = [mock_image1, mock_image2]
        
        # Setup corretor de imagens
        mock_corrector = Mock()
        processed_image1 = Mock(spec=Image.Image)
        processed_image2 = Mock(spec=Image.Image)
        mock_corrector.process_pil_image.side_effect = [processed_image1, processed_image2]
        mock_image_corrector.return_value = mock_corrector
        
        with patch('builtins.print'):
            service = OCRService()
            result = service.convert_pdf_to_images("/path/to/test.pdf", "LPCO123")
        
        # Verificar resultado
        assert result == ["/tmp/page_1_LPCO123.png", "/tmp/page_2_LPCO123.png"]
        
        # Verificar chamadas
        mock_convert.assert_called_once_with("/path/to/test.pdf", dpi=300)
        assert mock_corrector.process_pil_image.call_count == 2
        processed_image1.save.assert_called_once_with("/tmp/page_1_LPCO123.png", "PNG")
        processed_image2.save.assert_called_once_with("/tmp/page_2_LPCO123.png", "PNG")
    
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.convert_from_path')
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.DataConsolidator')
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.ImageCorrector')
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.get_ocr_provider')
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.get_file_manager')
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.get_config')
    def test_convert_pdf_to_images_error(self, mock_get_config, mock_get_file_manager,
                                       mock_get_ocr_provider, mock_image_corrector,
                                       mock_data_consolidator, mock_convert):
        """Testa erro na conversão de PDF para imagens."""
        mock_get_config.return_value = Mock(dpi=300)
        mock_get_file_manager.return_value = Mock()
        mock_get_ocr_provider.return_value = Mock()
        
        mock_convert.side_effect = Exception("Conversion failed")
        
        with patch('builtins.print') as mock_print:
            service = OCRService()
            
            with pytest.raises(Exception, match="Conversion failed"):
                service.convert_pdf_to_images("/path/to/invalid.pdf", "LPCO123")
            
            mock_print.assert_any_call("[OCR] Erro ao converter PDF para imagens: Conversion failed")


class TestProcessImages:
    """Testes para processamento de imagens com OCR."""
    
    def setup_method(self):
        """Setup para cada teste."""
        # Reset singleton
        OCRService._instance = None
        OCRService._config = None
        OCRService._ocr_provider = None
    
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.DataConsolidator')
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.ImageCorrector')
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.get_ocr_provider')
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.get_file_manager')
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.get_config')
    def test_process_images_success(self, mock_get_config, mock_get_file_manager,
                                  mock_get_ocr_provider, mock_image_corrector,
                                  mock_data_consolidator):
        """Testa processamento bem-sucedido de imagens."""
        # Setup OCR provider mock
        mock_provider = Mock()
        mock_provider.readtext.side_effect = [
            [([0, 0, 100, 50], "Acidez Livre:", 0.95), ([0, 50, 100, 100], "O,25%", 0.90)],
            [([0, 0, 100, 50], "C18:1 Oléico:", 0.92), ([0, 50, 100, 100], "75,2%", 0.88)]
        ]
        mock_get_ocr_provider.return_value = mock_provider
        
        # Setup consolidator mock
        mock_consolidator = Mock()
        mock_consolidator.consolidate_fragmented_data.return_value = "Texto consolidado"
        mock_data_consolidator.return_value = mock_consolidator
        
        mock_get_config.return_value = Mock(ocr_provider="easy", debug_ocr=False)
        mock_get_file_manager.return_value = Mock()
        
        with patch('builtins.print'):
            service = OCRService()
            result = service.process_images(["/path/img1.png", "/path/img2.png"])
        
        assert result == "Texto consolidado"
        
        # Verificar chamadas OCR
        assert mock_provider.readtext.call_count == 2
        mock_provider.readtext.assert_any_call("/path/img1.png")
        mock_provider.readtext.assert_any_call("/path/img2.png")
        
        # Verificar consolidação
        mock_consolidator.consolidate_fragmented_data.assert_called_once()
    
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.DataConsolidator')
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.ImageCorrector')
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.get_file_manager')
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.get_config')
    def test_process_images_no_provider(self, mock_get_config, mock_get_file_manager,
                                      mock_image_corrector, mock_data_consolidator):
        """Testa processamento sem provedor OCR."""
        mock_get_config.return_value = Mock(ocr_provider="easy", debug_ocr=False)
        mock_get_file_manager.return_value = Mock()
        
        with patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.get_ocr_provider', side_effect=Exception()), \
             patch('builtins.print'):
            
            service = OCRService()
            
            with pytest.raises(RuntimeError, match="Provedor OCR não está disponível"):
                service.process_images(["/path/img1.png"])
    
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.DataConsolidator')
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.ImageCorrector')
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.get_ocr_provider')
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.get_file_manager')
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.get_config')
    def test_process_images_with_ocr_error(self, mock_get_config, mock_get_file_manager,
                                         mock_get_ocr_provider, mock_image_corrector,
                                         mock_data_consolidator):
        """Testa processamento com erro no OCR (deve continuar com outras imagens)."""
        # Setup OCR provider com erro na primeira imagem
        mock_provider = Mock()
        mock_provider.readtext.side_effect = [
            Exception("OCR failed for image 1"),
            [([0, 0, 100, 50], "Texto válido", 0.95)]
        ]
        mock_get_ocr_provider.return_value = mock_provider
        
        mock_consolidator = Mock()
        mock_consolidator.consolidate_fragmented_data.return_value = "Texto consolidado"
        mock_data_consolidator.return_value = mock_consolidator
        
        mock_get_config.return_value = Mock(ocr_provider="easy", debug_ocr=False)
        mock_get_file_manager.return_value = Mock()
        
        with patch('builtins.print') as mock_print:
            service = OCRService()
            result = service.process_images(["/path/img1.png", "/path/img2.png"])
        
        assert result == "Texto consolidado"
        mock_print.assert_any_call("[OCR] Aviso: Falha ao processar imagem /path/img1.png: OCR failed for image 1")


class TestProcessSinglePage:
    """Testes para processamento de página única."""
    
    def setup_method(self):
        """Setup para cada teste."""
        # Reset singleton
        OCRService._instance = None
        OCRService._config = None
        OCRService._ocr_provider = None
    
    @patch('os.path.exists')
    @patch('os.remove')
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.convert_from_path')
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.DataConsolidator')
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.ImageCorrector')
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.get_ocr_provider')
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.get_file_manager')
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.get_config')
    def test_process_single_page_success(self, mock_get_config, mock_get_file_manager,
                                       mock_get_ocr_provider, mock_image_corrector,
                                       mock_data_consolidator, mock_convert,
                                       mock_remove, mock_exists):
        """Testa processamento bem-sucedido de página única."""
        # Setup mocks
        mock_config = Mock()
        mock_config.dpi = 300
        mock_get_config.return_value = mock_config
        
        mock_file_manager = Mock()
        mock_file_manager.get_temp_image_path.return_value = "/tmp/page_2.png"
        mock_get_file_manager.return_value = mock_file_manager
        
        mock_provider = Mock()
        mock_provider.readtext.return_value = [([0, 0, 100, 50], "Test Text", 0.95)]
        mock_get_ocr_provider.return_value = mock_provider
        
        # Criar imagem PIL mock
        mock_image = Mock(spec=Image.Image)
        mock_convert.return_value = [mock_image]
        
        # Setup corretor de imagens
        mock_corrector = Mock()
        processed_image = Mock(spec=Image.Image)
        mock_corrector.process_pil_image.return_value = processed_image
        mock_image_corrector.return_value = mock_corrector
        
        # Setup consolidator
        mock_consolidator = Mock()
        mock_consolidator.consolidate_fragmented_data.return_value = "Test Text Consolidado"
        mock_data_consolidator.return_value = mock_consolidator
        
        mock_exists.return_value = True
        
        with patch('builtins.print'):
            service = OCRService()
            result = service.process_single_page("/path/to/test.pdf", 2)
        
        assert "Test Text" in result
        
        # Verificar chamadas
        mock_convert.assert_called_once_with("/path/to/test.pdf", dpi=300, first_page=2, last_page=2)
        mock_corrector.process_pil_image.assert_called_once_with(mock_image)
        processed_image.save.assert_called_once_with("/tmp/page_2.png", "PNG")
        mock_exists.assert_called_once_with("/tmp/page_2.png")
        mock_remove.assert_called_once_with("/tmp/page_2.png")
    
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.convert_from_path')
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.DataConsolidator')
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.ImageCorrector')
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.get_ocr_provider')
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.get_file_manager')
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.get_config')
    def test_process_single_page_empty_images(self, mock_get_config, mock_get_file_manager,
                                            mock_get_ocr_provider, mock_image_corrector,
                                            mock_data_consolidator, mock_convert):
        """Testa processamento quando conversão retorna lista vazia."""
        mock_config = Mock()
        mock_config.dpi = 300
        mock_get_config.return_value = mock_config
        
        mock_get_file_manager.return_value = Mock()
        mock_get_ocr_provider.return_value = Mock()
        
        mock_convert.return_value = []  # Lista vazia
        
        with patch('builtins.print') as mock_print:
            service = OCRService()
            result = service.process_single_page("/path/to/test.pdf", 1)
        
        assert result == ""
        mock_print.assert_any_call("[OCR] ERRO: Conversão da página 1 retornou lista vazia!")
    
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.convert_from_path')
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.DataConsolidator')
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.ImageCorrector')
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.get_ocr_provider')
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.get_file_manager')
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.get_config')
    def test_process_single_page_error(self, mock_get_config, mock_get_file_manager,
                                     mock_get_ocr_provider, mock_image_corrector,
                                     mock_data_consolidator, mock_convert):
        """Testa tratamento de erro no processamento de página única."""
        mock_get_config.return_value = Mock(dpi=300)
        mock_get_file_manager.return_value = Mock()
        mock_get_ocr_provider.return_value = Mock()
        
        mock_convert.side_effect = Exception("Page conversion failed")
        
        with patch('builtins.print') as mock_print:
            service = OCRService()
            result = service.process_single_page("/path/to/test.pdf", 1)
        
        assert result == ""
        mock_print.assert_any_call("[OCR] Erro ao processar página 1: Page conversion failed")


class TestTextCorrections:
    """Testes para correções de texto OCR."""
    
    def setup_method(self):
        """Setup para cada teste."""
        # Reset singleton
        OCRService._instance = None
        OCRService._config = None
        OCRService._ocr_provider = None
    
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.DataConsolidator')
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.ImageCorrector')
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.get_ocr_provider')
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.get_file_manager')
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.get_config')
    def test_apply_text_corrections_basic(self, mock_get_config, mock_get_file_manager,
                                        mock_get_ocr_provider, mock_image_corrector,
                                        mock_data_consolidator):
        """Testa correções básicas de texto OCR."""
        mock_get_config.return_value = Mock(ocr_provider="easy", debug_ocr=False)
        mock_get_file_manager.return_value = Mock()
        mock_get_ocr_provider.return_value = Mock()
        
        with patch('builtins.print'):
            service = OCRService()
            
            # Teste de correção 0/O
            text = "Acidez Livre: O,25%\nC18:O Oleico: 75,2%"
            result = service._apply_text_corrections(text)
            
            # Verificar que aplicou algumas correções (implementação pode variar)
            assert isinstance(result, str)
            assert "Acidez Livre:" in result
    
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.DataConsolidator')
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.ImageCorrector')
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.get_ocr_provider')
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.get_file_manager')
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.get_config')
    def test_apply_text_corrections_empty_lines(self, mock_get_config, mock_get_file_manager,
                                               mock_get_ocr_provider, mock_image_corrector,
                                               mock_data_consolidator):
        """Testa correções com linhas vazias."""
        mock_get_config.return_value = Mock(ocr_provider="easy", debug_ocr=False)
        mock_get_file_manager.return_value = Mock()
        mock_get_ocr_provider.return_value = Mock()
        
        with patch('builtins.print'):
            service = OCRService()
            
            text = "Linha 1\n\n\nLinha 4"
            result = service._apply_text_corrections(text)
            
            lines = result.split('\n')
            assert len(lines) == 4
            assert lines[1] == ""  # Linha vazia preservada
            assert lines[2] == ""  # Linha vazia preservada
    
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.DataConsolidator')
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.ImageCorrector')
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.get_ocr_provider')
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.get_file_manager')
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.get_config')
    def test_correct_zero_o_confusion(self, mock_get_config, mock_get_file_manager,
                                    mock_get_ocr_provider, mock_image_corrector,
                                    mock_data_consolidator):
        """Testa correção específica de confusão 0/O."""
        mock_get_config.return_value = Mock(ocr_provider="easy", debug_ocr=False)
        mock_get_file_manager.return_value = Mock()
        mock_get_ocr_provider.return_value = Mock()
        
        with patch('builtins.print'):
            service = OCRService()
            
            # Testar casos específicos
            test_cases = [
                ("O", "O"),  # Token muito curto, não altera
                ("C18O", "C18O"),  # Pode ou não alterar dependendo da implementação
                ("OO1", "OO1"),  # Pode ou não alterar dependendo da implementação
            ]
            
            for input_token, _ in test_cases:
                result = service._correct_zero_o_confusion(input_token)
                assert isinstance(result, str)
                assert len(result) >= len(input_token.replace('O', ''))  # Não remove caracteres
    
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.DataConsolidator')
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.ImageCorrector')
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.get_ocr_provider')
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.get_file_manager')
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.get_config')
    def test_helper_methods(self, mock_get_config, mock_get_file_manager,
                          mock_get_ocr_provider, mock_image_corrector,
                          mock_data_consolidator):
        """Testa métodos auxiliares de correção."""
        mock_get_config.return_value = Mock(ocr_provider="easy", debug_ocr=False)
        mock_get_file_manager.return_value = Mock()
        mock_get_ocr_provider.return_value = Mock()
        
        with patch('builtins.print'):
            service = OCRService()
            
            # Test _get_adjacent_char
            chars = ['A', 'B', 'C', 'D']
            assert service._get_adjacent_char(chars, 1, -1) == 'A'  # B -> A
            assert service._get_adjacent_char(chars, 1, 1) == 'C'   # B -> C
            assert service._get_adjacent_char(chars, 0, -1) is None  # Fora dos limites
            assert service._get_adjacent_char(chars, 3, 1) is None   # Fora dos limites
            
            # Test _is_double_o_sequence
            test_chars = ['C', 'O', 'O', '1']
            assert service._is_double_o_sequence(test_chars, 1) is True
            assert service._is_double_o_sequence(test_chars, 0) is False
            assert service._is_double_o_sequence(test_chars, 2) is False
            
            # Test _should_be_numeric_context
            assert service._should_be_numeric_context('A', '1') is True   # Letra + número
            assert service._should_be_numeric_context('1', '2') is True   # Número + número
            assert service._should_be_numeric_context('A', None) is True  # Letra + fim
            assert service._should_be_numeric_context('A', 'B') is False  # Letra + letra


class TestOCRServiceIntegration:
    """Testes de integração para OCRService."""
    
    def setup_method(self):
        """Setup para cada teste."""
        # Reset singleton
        OCRService._instance = None
        OCRService._config = None
        OCRService._ocr_provider = None
    
    @patch('os.path.exists')
    @patch('os.remove')
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.convert_from_path')
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.DataConsolidator')
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.ImageCorrector')
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.get_ocr_provider')
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.get_file_manager')
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.get_config')
    def test_full_pdf_processing_workflow(self, mock_get_config, mock_get_file_manager,
                                         mock_get_ocr_provider, mock_image_corrector,
                                         mock_data_consolidator, mock_convert,
                                         mock_remove, mock_exists):
        """Testa fluxo completo de processamento de PDF."""
        # Setup completo de mocks
        mock_config = Mock()
        mock_config.dpi = 200
        mock_config.ocr_provider = "easy"
        mock_config.debug_ocr = False
        mock_get_config.return_value = mock_config
        
        mock_file_manager = Mock()
        mock_file_manager.get_temp_image_path.side_effect = [
            "/tmp/page_1_LPCO001.png",
            "/tmp/page_1.png"
        ]
        mock_get_file_manager.return_value = mock_file_manager
        
        mock_provider = Mock()
        mock_provider.provider_name = "EasyOCR"
        mock_provider.readtext.return_value = [
            ([0, 0, 100, 50], "Laboratorio: MAPA", 0.95),
            ([0, 50, 100, 100], "Acidez Livre: O,25%", 0.90)
        ]
        mock_get_ocr_provider.return_value = mock_provider
        
        # Criar imagem PIL mock
        mock_image = Mock(spec=Image.Image)
        mock_convert.side_effect = [
            [mock_image],  # convert_pdf_to_images
            [mock_image]   # process_single_page
        ]
        
        # Setup corretor de imagens
        mock_corrector = Mock()
        processed_image = Mock(spec=Image.Image)
        mock_corrector.process_pil_image.return_value = processed_image
        mock_image_corrector.return_value = mock_corrector
        
        # Setup consolidator
        mock_consolidator = Mock()
        mock_consolidator.consolidate_fragmented_data.return_value = "Texto final consolidado"
        mock_data_consolidator.return_value = mock_consolidator
        
        mock_exists.return_value = True
        
        with patch('builtins.print'):
            service = OCRService()
            
            # Testar conversão completa PDF -> imagens
            image_paths = service.convert_pdf_to_images("/path/laudo.pdf", "LPCO001")
            assert image_paths == ["/tmp/page_1_LPCO001.png"]
            
            # Testar processamento das imagens
            result = service.process_images(image_paths)
            assert result == "Texto final consolidado"
            
            # Testar processamento de página única
            single_result = service.process_single_page("/path/laudo.pdf", 1)
            assert single_result == "Texto final consolidado"


class TestOCRServiceErrorHandling:
    """Testes de tratamento de erro para OCRService."""
    
    def setup_method(self):
        """Setup para cada teste."""
        # Reset singleton
        OCRService._instance = None
        OCRService._config = None
        OCRService._ocr_provider = None
    
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.DataConsolidator')
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.ImageCorrector')  
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.get_ocr_provider')
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.get_file_manager')
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.get_config')
    def test_ocr_service_with_missing_dependencies(self, mock_get_config, mock_get_file_manager,
                                                  mock_get_ocr_provider, mock_image_corrector,
                                                  mock_data_consolidator):
        """Testa comportamento com dependências faltando."""
        mock_get_config.return_value = Mock(ocr_provider="easy", debug_ocr=False)
        mock_get_file_manager.return_value = Mock()
        
        # Simular falha na inicialização de componentes
        mock_image_corrector.side_effect = Exception("ImageCorrector failed")
        mock_get_ocr_provider.return_value = Mock()
        
        with patch('builtins.print'):
            with pytest.raises(Exception, match="ImageCorrector failed"):
                OCRService()
    
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.DataConsolidator')
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.ImageCorrector')
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.get_ocr_provider')
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.get_file_manager')
    @patch('app.services.ai.processors.ocr_service.get_config')
    def test_ocr_service_memory_management(self, mock_get_config, mock_get_file_manager,
                                         mock_get_ocr_provider, mock_image_corrector,
                                         mock_data_consolidator):
        """Testa gerenciamento de memória com múltiplas instâncias."""
        mock_get_config.return_value = Mock(ocr_provider="easy", debug_ocr=False)
        mock_get_file_manager.return_value = Mock()
        mock_get_ocr_provider.return_value = Mock(provider_name="EasyOCR")
        
        with patch('builtins.print'):
            # Criar múltiplas "instâncias" - deve ser a mesma devido ao singleton
            service1 = OCRService()
            service2 = get_ocr_service()
            service3 = OCRService()
            
            assert service1 is service2
            assert service2 is service3
            assert OCRService._instance is service1

            assert mock_get_ocr_provider.call_count <= 2  # Inicial + possível fallback

class TestConvertExcelToPdfLibreoffice:
    """Testes para conversão Excel to PDF usando LibreOffice."""
    
    @patch('app.services.pdf_service._get_libreoffice_command')
    @patch('subprocess.run')
    def test_convert_excel_success(self, mock_subprocess, mock_get_cmd):
        """Testa conversão bem-sucedida de Excel para PDF."""
        mock_get_cmd.return_value = "libreoffice"
        mock_subprocess.return_value = Mock()
        
        excel_path = "/path/to/test.xlsx"
        
        convert_excel_to_pdf_libreoffice(excel_path)
        
        mock_get_cmd.assert_called_once()
        mock_subprocess.assert_called_once_with([
            "libreoffice",
            "--headless",
            "--convert-to", "pdf",
            excel_path
        ], check=True)
    
    @patch('app.services.pdf_service._get_libreoffice_command')
    def test_convert_excel_no_libreoffice_command(self, mock_get_cmd):
        """Testa erro quando LibreOffice não é encontrado."""
        mock_get_cmd.return_value = None
        
        excel_path = "/path/to/test.xlsx"
        
        with pytest.raises(FileNotFoundError, match="LibreOffice não encontrado"):
            convert_excel_to_pdf_libreoffice(excel_path)
    
    @patch('app.services.pdf_service._get_libreoffice_command')
    @patch('subprocess.run')
    def test_convert_excel_subprocess_error(self, mock_subprocess, mock_get_cmd):
        """Testa erro durante execução do subprocess."""
        mock_get_cmd.return_value = "libreoffice"
        mock_subprocess.side_effect = subprocess.CalledProcessError(1, "libreoffice")
        
        excel_path = "/path/to/test.xlsx"
        
        with pytest.raises(subprocess.CalledProcessError):
            convert_excel_to_pdf_libreoffice(excel_path)
    
    @patch('app.services.pdf_service._get_libreoffice_command')
    @patch('subprocess.run')
    def test_convert_excel_with_macos_path(self, mock_subprocess, mock_get_cmd):
        """Testa conversão usando caminho específico do macOS."""
        macos_path = "/Applications/LibreOffice.app/Contents/MacOS/soffice"
        mock_get_cmd.return_value = macos_path
        mock_subprocess.return_value = Mock()
        
        excel_path = "/path/to/test.xlsx"
        
        convert_excel_to_pdf_libreoffice(excel_path)
        
        mock_subprocess.assert_called_once_with([
            macos_path,
            "--headless",
            "--convert-to", "pdf",
            excel_path
        ], check=True)


class TestGetLibreofficeCommand:
    """Testes para detecção do comando LibreOffice."""
    
    @patch('shutil.which')
    def test_get_libreoffice_command_standard(self, mock_which):
        """Testa detecção do comando LibreOffice padrão."""
        mock_which.side_effect = lambda cmd: "libreoffice" if cmd == "libreoffice" else None
        
        result = _get_libreoffice_command()
        
        assert result == "libreoffice"
        mock_which.assert_called_with("libreoffice")
    
    @patch('platform.system')
    @patch('os.path.exists')
    @patch('shutil.which')
    def test_get_libreoffice_command_macos(self, mock_which, mock_exists, mock_system):
        """Testa detecção do LibreOffice no macOS."""
        mock_which.return_value = None  # Não encontra comando padrão
        mock_system.return_value = "Darwin"
        mock_exists.return_value = True
        
        result = _get_libreoffice_command()
        
        expected_path = "/Applications/LibreOffice.app/Contents/MacOS/soffice"
        assert result == expected_path
        mock_exists.assert_called_with(expected_path)
    
    @patch('platform.system')
    @patch('os.path.exists') 
    @patch('shutil.which')
    def test_get_libreoffice_command_macos_not_found(self, mock_which, mock_exists, mock_system):
        """Testa quando LibreOffice não é encontrado no macOS."""
        mock_which.side_effect = [None, "soffice"]  # libreoffice não, soffice sim
        mock_system.return_value = "Darwin"
        mock_exists.return_value = False
        
        result = _get_libreoffice_command()
        
        assert result == "soffice"
    
    @patch('platform.system')
    @patch('os.path.exists')
    @patch('shutil.which')
    def test_get_libreoffice_command_windows_program_files(self, mock_which, mock_exists, mock_system):
        """Testa detecção do LibreOffice no Windows (Program Files)."""
        mock_which.return_value = None
        mock_system.return_value = "Windows"
        
        def mock_exists_side_effect(path):
            return path == "C:/Program Files/LibreOffice/program/soffice.exe"
        
        mock_exists.side_effect = mock_exists_side_effect
        
        result = _get_libreoffice_command()
        
        assert result == "C:/Program Files/LibreOffice/program/soffice.exe"
    
    @patch('platform.system')
    @patch('os.path.exists')
    @patch('shutil.which')
    def test_get_libreoffice_command_windows_program_files_x86(self, mock_which, mock_exists, mock_system):
        """Testa detecção do LibreOffice no Windows (Program Files x86)."""
        mock_which.return_value = None
        mock_system.return_value = "Windows"
        
        def mock_exists_side_effect(path):
            return path == "C:/Program Files (x86)/LibreOffice/program/soffice.exe"
        
        mock_exists.side_effect = mock_exists_side_effect
        
        result = _get_libreoffice_command()
        
        assert result == "C:/Program Files (x86)/LibreOffice/program/soffice.exe"
    
    @patch('platform.system')
    @patch('os.path.exists')
    @patch('shutil.which')
    def test_get_libreoffice_command_windows_not_found_fallback_soffice(self, mock_which, mock_exists, mock_system):
        """Testa fallback para soffice quando não encontra no Windows."""
        mock_which.side_effect = lambda cmd: "soffice" if cmd == "soffice" else None
        mock_system.return_value = "Windows"
        mock_exists.return_value = False
        
        result = _get_libreoffice_command()
        
        assert result == "soffice"
    
    @patch('platform.system')
    @patch('os.path.exists')
    @patch('shutil.which')
    def test_get_libreoffice_command_linux_fallback_soffice(self, mock_which, mock_exists, mock_system):
        """Testa fallback para soffice no Linux."""
        mock_which.side_effect = lambda cmd: "soffice" if cmd == "soffice" else None
        mock_system.return_value = "Linux"
        
        result = _get_libreoffice_command()
        
        assert result == "soffice"
    
    @patch('platform.system')
    @patch('os.path.exists')
    @patch('shutil.which')
    def test_get_libreoffice_command_not_found(self, mock_which, mock_exists, mock_system):
        """Testa quando LibreOffice não é encontrado em lugar nenhum."""
        mock_which.return_value = None
        mock_system.return_value = "Linux"
        mock_exists.return_value = False
        
        result = _get_libreoffice_command()
        
        assert result is None
    
    @patch('platform.system')
    @patch('os.path.exists')
    @patch('shutil.which') 
    def test_get_libreoffice_command_unknown_system(self, mock_which, mock_exists, mock_system):
        """Testa detecção em sistema operacional desconhecido."""
        mock_which.side_effect = [None, "soffice"]  # libreoffice não, soffice sim
        mock_system.return_value = "UnknownOS"
        
        result = _get_libreoffice_command()
        
        assert result == "soffice"


class TestPdfServiceIntegration:
    """Testes de integração para o serviço PDF."""
    
    @patch('app.services.pdf_service._get_libreoffice_command')
    @patch('subprocess.run')
    def test_end_to_end_conversion_flow(self, mock_subprocess, mock_get_cmd):
        """Testa fluxo completo de conversão."""
        mock_get_cmd.return_value = "libreoffice"
        mock_subprocess.return_value = Mock(returncode=0)
        
        excel_path = "/tmp/test_report.xlsx"
        
        # Deve executar sem erros
        convert_excel_to_pdf_libreoffice(excel_path)
        
        # Verifica se o comando foi montado corretamente
        expected_command = [
            "libreoffice",
            "--headless", 
            "--convert-to", "pdf",
            excel_path
        ]
        mock_subprocess.assert_called_once_with(expected_command, check=True)
    
    @patch('platform.system')
    def test_platform_detection_consistency(self, mock_system):
        """Testa consistência da detecção de plataforma."""
        test_cases = ['Linux', 'Darwin', 'Windows', 'FreeBSD']
        
        for system in test_cases:
            mock_system.return_value = system
            
            # Não deve gerar exceções
            with patch('shutil.which', return_value=None), \
                 patch('os.path.exists', return_value=False):
                result = _get_libreoffice_command()
                # Para sistemas não suportados, deve retornar None
                if system not in ['Linux', 'Darwin', 'Windows']:
                    assert result is None

class TestPdfName:
    """Testes para a função pdf_name que gera nomes únicos de arquivo."""
    
    @patch('app.controller.processamento_controller.datetime')
    def test_pdf_name_formats_correctly(self, mock_datetime):
        """Testa formatação correta do nome do arquivo PDF."""
        # Arrange
        mock_datetime.today.return_value.strftime.return_value = "15-01-2025"
        lpco = "BR2025123456"
        expected = "15-01-2025_BR2025123456"
        
        # Act
        result = pdf_name(lpco)
        
        # Assert
        assert result == expected
        mock_datetime.today.return_value.strftime.assert_called_once_with("%d-%m-%Y")
    
    @patch('app.controller.processamento_controller.datetime')
    def test_pdf_name_sanitizes_special_characters(self, mock_datetime):
        """Testa remoção de caracteres especiais do LPCO."""
        # Arrange
        mock_datetime.today.return_value.strftime.return_value = "15-01-2025"
        lpco_with_specials = "BR/2025-123.456#@!"
        expected = "15-01-2025_BR2025123456"
        
        # Act
        result = pdf_name(lpco_with_specials)
        
        # Assert
        assert result == expected
    
    @patch('app.controller.processamento_controller.datetime')
    def test_pdf_name_handles_empty_lpco(self, mock_datetime):
        """Testa comportamento com LPCO vazio após sanitização."""
        # Arrange
        mock_datetime.today.return_value.strftime.return_value = "15-01-2025"
        lpco_only_specials = "@#$%^&*()"
        expected = "15-01-2025_"
        
        # Act
        result = pdf_name(lpco_only_specials)
        
        # Assert
        assert result == expected


class TestSavePdf:
    """Testes para a função save_pdf que salva arquivos PDF."""
    
    def test_save_pdf_success(self, temp_dir, mock_upload_file):
        """Testa salvamento bem-sucedido de PDF válido."""
        # Arrange
        with patch('app.controller.processamento_controller.UPLOAD_DIR', str(temp_dir)):
            lpco = "TEST123"
            pdf_content = b"%PDF-1.4 test content"
            upload_file = mock_upload_file("test.pdf", pdf_content, "application/pdf")
            
            # Act
            file_path = save_pdf(lpco, upload_file)
            
            # Assert
            assert os.path.exists(file_path)
            assert file_path.startswith(str(temp_dir))
            assert file_path.endswith(".pdf")
            
            with open(file_path, "rb") as f:
                assert f.read() == pdf_content
    
    @pytest.mark.parametrize("filename,content_type,expected_error", [
        ("test.txt", "text/plain", "O arquivo precisa ser um PDF"),
        ("test.pdf", "image/png", "O arquivo precisa ser um PDF"),
        ("test.doc", "application/pdf", "O arquivo precisa ser um PDF"),
        ("test", "application/pdf", "O arquivo precisa ser um PDF"),
    ])
    def test_save_pdf_invalid_file_type(self, mock_upload_file, filename, content_type, expected_error):
        """Testa rejeição de arquivos não-PDF."""
        # Arrange
        upload_file = mock_upload_file(filename, b"content", content_type)
        
        # Act & Assert
        with pytest.raises(HTTPException) as exc_info:
            save_pdf("TEST", upload_file)
        
        assert exc_info.value.status_code == 400
        assert expected_error in exc_info.value.detail
    
    @patch('app.controller.processamento_controller.shutil.copyfileobj')
    def test_save_pdf_file_system_error(self, mock_copyfileobj, mock_upload_file):
        """Testa tratamento de erros do sistema de arquivos."""
        # Arrange
        mock_copyfileobj.side_effect = OSError("Disk full")
        upload_file = mock_upload_file("test.pdf", b"content", "application/pdf")
        
        # Act & Assert
        with pytest.raises(OSError, match="Disk full"):
            save_pdf("TEST", upload_file)


class TestExtractPdfData:
    """Testes para a função extract_pdf_data que orquestra extração de dados."""
    
    @patch('app.controller.processamento_controller.convert_pdf_to_images_and_extract_data')
    @patch('app.controller.processamento_controller.save_pdf')
    def test_extract_pdf_data_success(self, mock_save_pdf, mock_convert, mock_upload_file):
        """Testa extração bem-sucedida de dados do PDF."""
        # Arrange
        mock_save_pdf.return_value = "/path/to/saved.pdf"
        mock_convert.return_value = ({"param": "value"}, {"info": "data"})
        
        lpco = "TEST123"
        upload_file = mock_upload_file("test.pdf", b"content", "application/pdf")
        
        # Act
        result = extract_pdf_data(lpco, upload_file)
        
        # Assert
        assert result == {
            "quimico": {"param": "value"},
            "cabecalho": {"info": "data"}
        }
        
        mock_save_pdf.assert_called_once_with(lpco, upload_file)
        mock_convert.assert_called_once_with("/path/to/saved.pdf", "TEST123")
    
    @patch('app.controller.processamento_controller.convert_pdf_to_images_and_extract_data')
    @patch('app.controller.processamento_controller.save_pdf')
    def test_extract_pdf_data_ai_service_failure(self, mock_save_pdf, mock_convert, mock_upload_file):
        """Testa comportamento quando serviço de IA falha."""
        # Arrange
        mock_save_pdf.return_value = "/path/to/saved.pdf"
        mock_convert.side_effect = RuntimeError("AI service failed")
        
        upload_file = mock_upload_file("test.pdf", b"content", "application/pdf")
        
        # Act & Assert
        with pytest.raises(RuntimeError, match="AI service failed"):
            extract_pdf_data("TEST", upload_file)
    
    @patch('app.controller.processamento_controller.save_pdf')
    def test_extract_pdf_data_save_failure_propagates(self, mock_save_pdf, mock_upload_file):
        """Testa que falhas no salvamento são propagadas."""
        # Arrange
        mock_save_pdf.side_effect = HTTPException(status_code=400, detail="Invalid file")
        upload_file = mock_upload_file("test.pdf", b"content", "application/pdf")
        
        # Act & Assert
        with pytest.raises(HTTPException) as exc_info:
            extract_pdf_data("TEST", upload_file)
        
        assert exc_info.value.status_code == 400
        assert "Invalid file" in exc_info.value.detail


class TestCreateSheetsAndSavePdf:
    """Testes para a função create_sheets_and_save_pdf que gera relatório final."""
    
    @patch('app.controller.processamento_controller.update_excel')
    @patch('app.controller.processamento_controller.convert_excel_to_pdf_libreoffice')
    def test_create_sheets_and_save_pdf_success(self, mock_convert_excel, mock_update_excel, temp_dir):
        """Testa geração bem-sucedida de relatório PDF final."""
        # Arrange
        lpco = "TEST123"
        chem_data = {"acidez": "0.5"}
        sec_data = {"lote": "L123"}
        
        # Simular arquivos criados pelas dependências
        with patch('app.controller.processamento_controller.pdf_name', return_value="test-file"):
            expected_pdf = temp_dir / "test-file.pdf"
            expected_xlsx = temp_dir / "test-file.xlsx"
            
            # Criar arquivos que a função espera
            expected_pdf.write_bytes(b"pdf content")
            expected_xlsx.write_bytes(b"excel content")
            
            # Mockar working directory
            with patch('os.getcwd', return_value=str(temp_dir)):
                # Act
                response = create_sheets_and_save_pdf(lpco, chem_data, sec_data)
        
        # Assert
        assert isinstance(response, FileResponse)
        assert response.headers["X-Lpco"] == lpco
        assert "X-Link-Sharepoint" in response.headers
        
        # Verificar chamadas das dependências
        mock_update_excel.assert_called_once_with(chem_data, sec_data, "test-file")
        mock_convert_excel.assert_called_once_with("test-file.xlsx")
    
    def test_create_sheets_and_save_pdf_cleanup_task(self, temp_dir):
        """Testa se a tarefa de cleanup é configurada corretamente."""
        # Arrange
        with patch('app.controller.processamento_controller.update_excel'), \
             patch('app.controller.processamento_controller.convert_excel_to_pdf_libreoffice'), \
             patch('app.controller.processamento_controller.pdf_name', return_value="cleanup-test"), \
             patch('os.getcwd', return_value=str(temp_dir)):
            
            pdf_file = temp_dir / "cleanup-test.pdf"
            xlsx_file = temp_dir / "cleanup-test.xlsx"
            
            # Criar arquivos
            pdf_file.write_bytes(b"pdf")
            xlsx_file.write_bytes(b"xlsx")
            
            # Act
            response = create_sheets_and_save_pdf("TEST", {}, {})
        
        # Assert
        assert isinstance(response.background, BackgroundTasks)
        assert len(response.background.tasks) == 1
        
        # Executar tarefa de cleanup manualmente
        assert pdf_file.exists()
        assert xlsx_file.exists()
        
        task = response.background.tasks[0]
        # Execute cleanup in the same context as the test (with mocked cwd and path operations)
        with patch('os.getcwd', return_value=str(temp_dir)), \
             patch('os.path.exists') as mock_exists, \
             patch('os.remove') as mock_remove:
            
            # Mock exists to check files in temp_dir
            def exists_side_effect(path):
                if path == "cleanup-test.pdf":
                    return pdf_file.exists()
                elif path == "cleanup-test.xlsx":
                    return xlsx_file.exists()
                return False
            
            # Mock remove to actually remove files from temp_dir
            def remove_side_effect(path):
                if path == "cleanup-test.pdf":
                    pdf_file.unlink(missing_ok=True)
                elif path == "cleanup-test.xlsx":
                    xlsx_file.unlink(missing_ok=True)
            
            mock_exists.side_effect = exists_side_effect
            mock_remove.side_effect = remove_side_effect
            
            task.func(*task.args, **task.kwargs)
        
        # Verificar que arquivos foram removidos
        assert not pdf_file.exists()
        assert not xlsx_file.exists()
    
    @patch('app.controller.processamento_controller.update_excel')
    def test_create_sheets_and_save_pdf_excel_failure(self, mock_update_excel):
        """Testa comportamento quando atualização do Excel falha."""
        # Arrange
        mock_update_excel.side_effect = Exception("Excel update failed")
        
        # Act & Assert
        with pytest.raises(Exception, match="Excel update failed"):
            create_sheets_and_save_pdf("TEST", {}, {})
    
    @patch('app.controller.processamento_controller.update_excel')
    @patch('app.controller.processamento_controller.convert_excel_to_pdf_libreoffice')
    def test_create_sheets_and_save_pdf_conversion_failure(self, mock_convert, mock_update):
        """Testa comportamento quando conversão para PDF falha."""
        # Arrange
        mock_convert.side_effect = Exception("PDF conversion failed")
        
        # Act & Assert
        with pytest.raises(Exception, match="PDF conversion failed"):
            create_sheets_and_save_pdf("TEST", {}, {})
    
    def test_cleanup_task_handles_missing_files(self, temp_dir):
        """Testa que cleanup não falha se arquivos já foram removidos."""
        # Arrange
        with patch('app.controller.processamento_controller.update_excel'), \
             patch('app.controller.processamento_controller.convert_excel_to_pdf_libreoffice'), \
             patch('app.controller.processamento_controller.pdf_name', return_value="missing-files"):
            
            with patch('os.getcwd', return_value=str(temp_dir)):
                response = create_sheets_and_save_pdf("TEST", {}, {})
        
        # Act - executar cleanup sem criar arquivos
        task = response.background.tasks[0]
        
        # Assert - não deve levantar exceção
        try:
            task.func(*task.args, **task.kwargs)
        except Exception as e:
            pytest.fail(f"Cleanup task falhou com arquivos inexistentes: {e}")
    
    @patch('os.remove')
    def test_cleanup_task_handles_permission_errors(self, mock_remove, temp_dir):
        """Testa que cleanup trata erros de permissão graciosamente."""
        # Arrange
        mock_remove.side_effect = PermissionError("Permission denied")
        
        with patch('app.controller.processamento_controller.update_excel'), \
             patch('app.controller.processamento_controller.convert_excel_to_pdf_libreoffice'), \
             patch('app.controller.processamento_controller.pdf_name', return_value="permission-test"):
            
            # Criar arquivos reais
            pdf_file = temp_dir / "permission-test.pdf"
            xlsx_file = temp_dir / "permission-test.xlsx"
            pdf_file.write_bytes(b"pdf")
            xlsx_file.write_bytes(b"xlsx")
            
            with patch('os.getcwd', return_value=str(temp_dir)), \
                 patch('os.path.exists', return_value=True):
                response = create_sheets_and_save_pdf("TEST", {}, {})
        
        # Act - executar cleanup que falhará
        task = response.background.tasks[0]
        
        # Assert - não deve levantar exceção, deve imprimir erro
        try:
            task.func(*task.args, **task.kwargs)
        except Exception as e:
            pytest.fail(f"Cleanup task não tratou erro de permissão: {e}")

class TestProcessamentoIntegration:
    """Testes de integração para fluxo completo de processamento."""
    
    @patch('app.controller.processamento_controller.convert_pdf_to_images_and_extract_data')
    @patch('app.controller.processamento_controller.update_excel')
    @patch('app.controller.processamento_controller.convert_excel_to_pdf_libreoffice')
    def test_full_processing_flow(self, mock_pdf_convert, mock_excel_update, mock_ai_extract, 
                                  temp_dir, mock_upload_file):
        """Testa o fluxo completo: upload → extração → processamento → download."""
        # Arrange
        mock_ai_extract.return_value = ({"param": "value"}, {"info": "data"})
        
        lpco = "INTEGRATION_TEST"
        upload_file = mock_upload_file("test.pdf", b"%PDF content", "application/pdf")
        
        with patch('app.controller.processamento_controller.UPLOAD_DIR', str(temp_dir)):
            # Act - Etapa 1: Extração
            extract_result = extract_pdf_data(lpco, upload_file)
            
            # Assert - Etapa 1
            assert extract_result["quimico"] == {"param": "value"}
            assert extract_result["cabecalho"] == {"info": "data"}
            
            # Act - Etapa 2: Processamento
            with patch('app.controller.processamento_controller.pdf_name', return_value="integration-test"):
                # Criar arquivos que serão gerados
                pdf_file = temp_dir / "integration-test.pdf"
                xlsx_file = temp_dir / "integration-test.xlsx"
                pdf_file.write_bytes(b"final pdf")
                xlsx_file.write_bytes(b"excel data")
                
                with patch('os.getcwd', return_value=str(temp_dir)):
                    response = create_sheets_and_save_pdf(
                        lpco, extract_result["quimico"], extract_result["cabecalho"]
                    )
            
            # Assert - Etapa 2
            assert isinstance(response, FileResponse)
            assert response.headers["X-Lpco"] == lpco
            
            # Verificar que todas as dependências foram chamadas
            mock_ai_extract.assert_called_once()
            mock_excel_update.assert_called_once()
            mock_pdf_convert.assert_called_once()"""Testes para SharePointService - Upload de arquivos para SharePoint."""

class TestSavePdfSharepoint:
    """Testes para upload de PDF para SharePoint."""
    
    @patch('app.services.sharepoint_service.ClientContext')
    @patch('app.services.sharepoint_service.UserCredential')
    @patch('builtins.open', new_callable=mock_open, read_data=b'fake pdf content')
    def test_save_pdf_sharepoint_success(self, mock_file, mock_credential, mock_context):
        """Testa upload bem-sucedido de PDF para SharePoint."""
        # Mock do contexto SharePoint
        mock_ctx_instance = Mock()
        mock_context.return_value = mock_ctx_instance
        mock_ctx_instance.with_credentials.return_value = mock_ctx_instance
        
        # Mock da web e folder
        mock_web = Mock()
        mock_ctx_instance.web = mock_web
        mock_web.get.return_value = mock_web
        # Make sure both execute_query calls are tracked on the same object
        mock_web.execute_query = mock_ctx_instance.execute_query
        
        mock_folder = Mock()
        mock_web.get_folder_by_server_relative_url.return_value = mock_folder
        
        file_name = "test_report.pdf"
        
        result = save_pdf_sharepoint(file_name)
        
        # Verifica se o contexto foi criado corretamente
        expected_site_url = "https://agromapa.sharepoint.com/sites/CentraldeAzeitedeOliva/"
        mock_context.assert_called_once_with(expected_site_url)
        
        # Verifica se credenciais foram configuradas
        mock_ctx_instance.with_credentials.assert_called_once()
        
        # Verifica se arquivo foi aberto corretamente
        mock_file.assert_called_once_with(file_name, 'rb')
        
        # Verifica se upload foi executado
        mock_folder.upload_file.assert_called_once_with(file_name, b'fake pdf content')
        assert mock_ctx_instance.execute_query.call_count == 2  # Uma para web.get(), outra para upload
        
        # Verifica URL de retorno
        expected_url = f"https://agromapa.sharepoint.com/sites/CentraldeAzeitedeOliva/Documentos%20Compartilhados/Reposit%C3%B3rio%20Laudos%20Azeite%20OlivIA/teste-api-olivia/{file_name}"
        assert result == expected_url
